<userid>114246802996804666603< /userid>< name>
Hoyan Leung< /name>
< Date>
1618164116601<//Date>

5< /Rate>
< Review>
They are still serving up delicious food after all these years! I have been back countless times now and have ordered food through delivery during the strict COVID days in 2020. Their Gamjatang (pork bones with potatoes stew) is one of my favorite item to order on their menu. I love the taste of the sesame leaves and the rich pork bone broth flavored with sweetness from the napa cabbage. I also tried their dwaejiguk which is a pork jowl soup made with different cuts of pork ranging from pork belly to offals. Clean offal taste and the soup is thick and hearty. Adding in the salty shrimp and salt seasoning on the table make this soup so satisfying on a cold night.

The menu has changed from 2017 and they have added many more items now catering to the broader audiences. The Galbijjim is a generous serving of spicy braised beef short ribs that can fill 3 hungry stomaches. It's saucy with a good blend of sweet, savory, and spice. The beef flavor was nice and tender from slow cook and braise in the delicious sauce. Get it with the melted cheese on top! Their Ros√© Tteokbokki noodles is one of my newest favorite on their menu. It's a special twist to the normal tteokbokki where they added bacon, sausage, cream, cheese..? to the dish to give it that nice creamy and smoky taste as another layer on top. Really delicious and I kept going back to this dish while I'm enjoying my meal.

Other favorite items from this place, their galbitang (super satisfying), spicy cabbage galbitang (a sweeter and soy bean version of galbitang), soondae (they have perfected this and you eat with the salt and shrimpies on the table), korean fried chicken (KFC), bossam (pork belly wraps), and jokbal (pig trotters). The Korean cuisine here is one of the more authentic taste to the ones I've had in Korea! Service is kind and they care about the quality of the food they serve. Support your local businesses!

(all attached pictures are taken by me)</Review>

<Name>Sy Hwang< /Name><Time>1543030662958<//Time><rate>5</rate>< text>
We visited this place when it was pouring and the bubbling stews we ordered(soondae soup and neckbone hangover stew) hit the spot for a cold rainy day. I suspect most Korean-Americans like myself will find the food very authentic and comforting. Those who are new to this rustic type of Korean cuisine might need a bit more courage as there is a lot of offal in the soups and stews served here. For a safe choice, go for the galbi tang - a clear broth beef rib soup.</text>

<Text>We ordered the "Spicy Braised Beef Short Ribs" (see photo attached). That was enough for the two of us, the leftovers also fed us for lunch the next day. Needless to say, great value. If you're a party of 3,  I wouldn't hesitate to get that for the table. I loved gnazing on those bones. Warning: it can get messy eating this. The sauce was also the right amount of spicy for us.

<text>Moo Bong Ri has been in my radar ever since Von's Chicken departure. At first it was kinda hard to get in touch with them, but when I did, then language barrier set me back. Finally message came in telling me a low-key quiet soft opening is imminent. You see, in my profession there are areas that I look for in any place that deals with food. However, I'm not gonna exposed things of those elements today. How I perceive things, is that I don't want to know and don't need to know what I'm being told. I like things that are tangible in your face. So, when I'm told soup is good, I don't buy it till I try it myself. This blood sausage soup is pretty darn tasty IMHO. Bowl came with three banchan and a choice of white or brown wild rice. I chose the latter. It's piping hot and filled with one inch stubbly blood sausage pieces. Soup seems chock full of hearty nutrients with no visible oil sheen floating. You won't be disappointed here.<//text>< pics>

< Text>
During COVID-19, I called String Bead in hopes of finishing a birthday necklace on time. The owner kindly did all of my shopping (apparently I am out of control even over the phone when it comes to beads) and took payment over the phone, offered to set up a phone appointment to send me photos, asked customers to all sanitize upon entry (we were on the phone for a bit so I got to hear the activities), all customers happily complied, and then she met me curbside with my stuff. She had on a mask (properly) as did all customers leaving the shop. And she threw in some extra beads for me because she couldn't decide which ones I'd love best. String Bead for the win! ‚ù§Ô∏è Sidenote: this business was great before COVID-19 as well, always a great experience and amazing selection.</Text>

< review>
It's kind of hard for me to review this place because my first experience, which was in the late afternoon and arlier in the week and it was amazin.  I ordered a new dish on the menu called Mama D's pot roast.  That was as bold move on my part because I rarely will even order a meat dish from a restaurant, unless I happen to be at Alexanders Steak House or something equivalent to that. Ok, so, to my surprise it was perfect.  The carrots & celery were cooked perfect, just the right crunch still in them.  I'm not into soggy vegetables.  The meat was tender and lean.  Very good quality and cooked perfectly.   I was sold.  I kept talking about it for days, to whoever would listen.  Now FF to last night.  I sold my friend on the idea of going to Denny's to get this amazing Mama D's dish and I had such a bad experience.  They gave me something that slightly resembled what I had ordered earlier in the weak but it tasted horrible. It was salty and soggy and they gave me the wrong flavored milkshake and well, it just spiraled downward from there.  Granted it was midnight and they were probably ready to go home or something?  Anyways, I guess I will chop it up to inconsistent.  It's a gamble, but what isn't?< /review>

<userid>117153621738001397218< /userid><name>Shiv Kumar Ganesh<//name><Date>1525370512213< /Date><Rate>4<//Rate>< review>
This Denny's is on the El Camino Real and is same as any other Denny's. The staff is good and the place is mostly full. If you are planning for Friday and Saturday late night dinner or snack, keep in mind this place is packed with people. The other positive I see that this place is located near many other food joint and is not secluded. Parking space is not at all limited and this place is wheelchair accessible. Good for kids and adults. Remember you do have many options around this place if you are actually looking for something more elaborate. I like spending time here as it's close to my place. To add they have started a new menu where you can have a complete meal in $4,$6 etc. Do check that out!!</review>

<Name>Shelby Drakecliffe</Name><rate>4< /rate>< Text>
This was a good Denny's. We walked in and the hostess was clearly overworked but still so very friendly. She needed a raise. A big one.
We were seated at a comfortable booth. After chatting with the hostess we took a second to look at the menu. As soon as we opened them our waitress came over asking for us to order. A little taken aback (luckily we already knew what we wanted) we ordered and she hobbled away without a word. She was a very interesting elder woman. After delivering our food and the check (without asking if we wanted anything else) maybe ten minutes max later, she hobbled away and never came back. We enjoyed the food, it was tasty. I personally enjoy the dinner food at Denny's versus IHOP.
All in all, not a terrible decision and it was a tasty one at that.

I would recommend this place.</Text>

< text>
Best Denny's in Santa Clara

I've frequented many Denny's restaurants throughout the US, and this one is my new favorite.   The Service is Excellent, the Food is Excellent and the price is usually the same wherever you go (but still good).

I often get the Pot Roast and I can say that it has been a long time since I've considered ordering it again in the same sitting (to go).

Denny's always has great down-home favorites such as Pot Roast,  Country-Fried Steak, Spaghetti and Meatballs,  or Fish and Chips.  This restaurant does them all a service.

If you want a good idea of how amazing Denny's can be, eat at this location.<//text>
